 succeeded in 252ms:
rules_version = '2';

// =============================================================================
// Yugma Dukaan â€” Firestore Security Rules
// Per-shop scoping enforced on every read and write.
// Cross-tenant integrity test (cross_tenant_integrity_test.dart) MUST pass
// against this file on every PR â€” see ADR-012, R9.
//
// Sprint 1 scope: shopId scoping foundation + udhaar forbidden-field guard.
// Per-collection rules expand as Sprints 2â€“6 ship the corresponding stories.
// =============================================================================

service cloud.firestore {
  match /databases/{database}/documents {

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Helper functions
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    function isSignedIn() {
      return request.auth != null;
    }

    function isAnonymous() {
      return isSignedIn() && request.auth.token.firebase.sign_in_provider == 'anonymous';
    }

    function isPhoneVerified() {
      return isSignedIn() && request.auth.token.firebase.sign_in_provider == 'phone';
    }

    function isGoogleSignedIn() {
      return isSignedIn() && request.auth.token.firebase.sign_in_provider == 'google.com';
    }

    function callerShopId() {
      return request.auth.token.shopId;
    }

    function callerRole() {
      return request.auth.token.role;
    }

    function isShopMember(shopId) {
      return isSignedIn() && callerShopId() == shopId;
    }

    function isShopOperator(shopId) {
      return isShopMember(shopId) && isGoogleSignedIn() &&
        (callerRole() == 'bhaiya'
         || callerRole() == 'beta'
         || callerRole() == 'munshi');
    }

    // Phase 1.9 code review cleanup (Agent A finding #3, my pre-flag from
    // Phase 1.2 + 1.5): the operator role canonical vocabulary per SAD Â§5
    // + PRD + Brief is `bhaiya / beta / munshi`. Sprint 1.4 rules drifted
    // to `shopkeeper / son / munshi` â€” now aligned. The `signupNewOperator`
    // Cloud Function (ships Sprint 5+ per S4.2) must issue custom claims
    // with the same canonical names.

    function hasShopId(data) {
      return 'shopId' in data && data.shopId is string && data.shopId.size() > 0;
    }

    function shopIdMatches(shopId) {
      return hasShopId(request.resource.data)
          && request.resource.data.shopId == shopId;
    }

    // App Check enforcement: callable Cloud Functions enforce it via
    // `enforceAppCheck: true` in their onCall options (functions/src/
    // join_decision_circle.ts + generate_wa_me_link.ts). For Firestore +
    // Storage, App Check enforcement must be toggled on in the Firebase
    // Console (Project Settings â†’ App Check); the rule layer additionally
    // gates writes via the shopId token claim issued through auth flows.

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Shop lifecycle write-freeze helper (SAD Â§6 v1.0.4 + ADR-013 + R16/DPDP)
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Freezes ALL client writes as soon as shopLifecycle leaves "active".
    // Reads continue so customers/operators can access their data during the
    // DPDP retention window. Cloud Function 8 (shopDeactivationSweep) owns all
    // mutations while the shop is not active, including scoped deletion at
    // retention expiry. Every allow create/update/delete below AND-gates on
    // this helper per the non-optional I6.4 acceptance criterion.

    function shopIsWritable(shopId) {
      return exists(/databases/$(database)/documents/shops/$(shopId))
          && get(/databases/$(database)/documents/shops/$(shopId)).data.shopLifecycle == 'active';
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Role helpers (Phase 6 addition â€” aligned with SAD Â§6 naming)
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    function isOperatorOf(shopId) {
      return isShopOperator(shopId);
    }

    function isCustomerOf(shopId) {
      return isShopMember(shopId)
          && (isAnonymous() || isPhoneVerified());
    }

    // isBhaiyaOf(shopId) helper is intentionally NOT defined until a rule
    // actually needs to distinguish bhaiya from other operator roles
    // (currently isShopOperator covers all 3 roles uniformly). Add in
    // Sprint 3+ when S4.19 shop deactivation introduces bhaiya-only access.

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Forbidden vocabulary on Udhaar Ledger (ADR-010, RBI-defensive)
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    function hasForbiddenUdhaarFields(data) {
      return data.keys().hasAny([
        'interest',
        'interestRate',
        'overdueFee',
        'dueDate',
        'lendingTerms',
        'borrowerObligation',
        'defaultStatus',
        'collectionAttempt'
      ]);
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Catch-all default deny (REQUIRED â€” every collection must be explicit)
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    match /{document=**} {
      allow read, write: if false;
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // /shops/{shopId} â€” Shop document
    // Read: any signed-in user (including anonymous customers).
    // Anonymous users don't have shopId custom claims, but they need read
    // access for onboarding (B1.1) and browsing (B1.4/B1.5).
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    match /shops/{shopId} {
      allow read: if isSignedIn();
      allow create: if false; // shops are created server-side via admin SDK
      allow update: if isShopOperator(shopId) && shopIsWritable(shopId);
      allow delete: if false;

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/themeTokens/{docId} â€” multi-tenant theming (SAD Â§8)
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      match /themeTokens/{tokenDocId} {
        allow read: if isSignedIn();
        allow write: if isShopOperator(shopId) && shopIsWritable(shopId);
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/theme/{docId} â€” ShopThemeTokens current doc
      // Read by customer app at onboarding, written by shopkeeper settings.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      match /theme/{themeDocId} {
        allow read: if isSignedIn();
        allow write: if isShopOperator(shopId) && shopIsWritable(shopId);
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/featureFlags/{flagId} â€” Remote Config mirror
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      match /featureFlags/{flagId} {
        allow read: if isSignedIn();
        allow write: if false; // managed via Remote Config console only
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // Sub-collections expand in Sprints 2â€“6 as stories ship:
      //   projects/, customers/, chatThreads/, customerMemory/, decisionCircles/
      //
      // Phase 1.9 code review cleanup (Agent A finding #1): the Phase 1.5
      // shared models repos target these four sub-collections:
      //   inventory/, operators/, voiceNotes/, curatedShortlists/
      // Each needs an explicit match clause â€” otherwise they fall through
      // to the catch-all `allow read, write: if false` at line 122-124 and
      // every repo call fails with permission-denied at runtime. Baseline
      // rules below honor the documented access model; per-story stories
      // (B1.4, B1.5, B1.6, B1.12, S4.1, S4.3, S4.4, S4.5) may refine.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/operators/{uid} â€” per PRD S4.1 + S4.2.
      // Phase 1.9 add.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // Read: any signed-in operator of the shop (they may need to see
      //       other operators' roles for the S4.12 Settings list).
      // Create/update/delete: bhaiya-only (PRD S4.2 AC + SAD Â§5 permissions).
      // The `signupNewOperator` Cloud Function bypasses rules via admin SDK
      // for the very first operator (PRD PQ-C locked answer).

      match /operators/{operatorUid} {
        allow read: if isShopOperator(shopId);
        allow create, update: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                              && callerRole() == 'bhaiya'
                              && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                              && shopIsWritable(shopId);
        // Self-delete forbidden â€” enforces the "can't remove yourself as
        // bhaiya" posture in SAD Â§6 rule table. Bhaiya can delete OTHER
        // operators but not their own doc.
        allow delete: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                      && callerRole() == 'bhaiya'
                      && request.auth.uid != operatorUid
                      && shopIsWritable(shopId);
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/inventory/{skuId} â€” per PRD B1.4/B1.5/S4.3/S4.4/S4.5.
      // Phase 1.9 add.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // Read: public to any shop member (customer + operator) â€” SKUs are
      //       the catalog and must be visible to the customer app without
      //       extra auth gates.
      // Write: operator-only. B1.5 AC #7 notes `negotiableDownTo` is
      //       operator-only â€” the rule permits the field (the model has
      //       it) but customer reads never surface it in UI because the
      //       customer_app layer filters at render time.

      match /inventory/{skuId} {
        allow read: if isSignedIn();
        allow create, update: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                              && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                              && shopIsWritable(shopId);
        // Soft-delete only per PRD PQ-D â€” `isActive: false` via update.
        // Hard-delete forbidden in v1.
        allow delete: if false;
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/voiceNotes/{voiceNoteId} â€” per PRD B1.6/B1.7/B1.8/B1.10.
      // Phase 1.9 add.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // Read: public to any shop member â€” customers hear voice notes
      //       inline on B1.3 greeting, B1.5 SKU detail, B1.7 chat messages,
      //       B1.10 away banner. The audio file itself is in Cloud Storage
      //       and is governed by storage.rules (Sprint 3+ delta).
      // Write: operator-only. Only bhaiya + beta record voice notes per
      //       VoiceNoteAuthorRole enum. Munshi cannot.

      match /voiceNotes/{voiceNoteId} {
        allow read: if isSignedIn();
        allow create, update: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                              && callerRole() != 'munshi'
                              && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                              && shopIsWritable(shopId);
        // Voice notes are append-only per SAD Â§5 â€” no delete path.
        allow delete: if false;
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/curatedShortlists/{shortlistId} â€” per PRD B1.4/B1.12.
      // Phase 1.9 add.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // Read: public to any shop member â€” customers browse shortlists on
      //       B1.4.
      // Write: operator-only (bhaiya + beta can curate; munshi cannot).
      //       Finite cap of 6 per UX Spec Â§4.3 is enforced in the Dart
      //       CuratedShortlistRepo, not here â€” the rule layer doesn't know
      //       about the SKU count invariant (would require a list-length
      //       check on `request.resource.data.skuIdsInOrder` which is
      //       possible but adds rule complexity). Defense-in-depth via
      //       repo + security rule would require a future `hasAtMost(6)`
      //       helper; queued as Phase 2+ refinement.

      match /curatedShortlists/{shortlistId} {
        allow read: if isSignedIn();
        allow create, update: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                              && callerRole() != 'munshi'
                              && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                              && shopIsWritable(shopId);
        // Soft-delete via `isActive: false` update â€” hard delete forbidden.
        allow delete: if false;
      }

      // Sprint 1 stub for udhaarLedger â€” present so the cross-tenant test
      // can assert the forbidden-field guard works from day one. Writes
      // freeze automatically when shopLifecycle != 'active' per ADR-013.
      match /udhaarLedger/{ledgerId} {
        // Read: operator sees all; customer sees only own ledgers.
        allow read: if isSignedIn()
                    && (isShopOperator(shopId)
                        || resource.data.customerId == request.auth.uid);
        allow create: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                      && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                      && !hasForbiddenUdhaarFields(request.resource.data)
                      && shopIsWritable(shopId);
        // Update: operator only + forbidden vocabulary + RBI reminder caps.
        // reminderCountLifetime capped at 3 per PRD S4.10 AC #8.
        // reminderCadenceDays must be 7â€“30 per PRD S4.10 AC #9.
        // DI005 fix: guard checks with field existence to avoid null comparison
        // failures on ledgers created without these optional fields.
        allow update: if isShopOperator(shopId)
                      && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                      && !hasForbiddenUdhaarFields(request.resource.data)
                      && shopIsWritable(shopId)
                      && (!('reminderCountLifetime' in request.resource.data)
                          || request.resource.data.reminderCountLifetime <= 3)
                      && (!('reminderCadenceDays' in request.resource.data)
                          || (request.resource.data.reminderCadenceDays >= 7
                              && request.resource.data.reminderCadenceDays <= 30));
        allow delete: if false;
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // v1.0.4 patch â€” feedback sub-collection (SAD Â§6 + S4.17 NPS + burnout)
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // Customers create their own customer_nps / customer_csat documents.
      // Operators create their own shopkeeper_burnout_self_report /
      // shopkeeper_usage_sample documents. All feedback is immutable after
      // create â€” no update, no delete. Reads: operators see everything in
      // their shop; customers see only their own submissions.

      match /feedback/{feedbackId} {
        allow read: if isSignedIn()
                    && (isShopOperator(shopId)
                        || (resource.data.authorUid == request.auth.uid
                            && resource.data.authorRole == 'customer'));
        // Uses shopIdMatches() helper for consistency with udhaarLedger
        // rule. Sprint 2.3 cleanup per code review finding Agent A ðŸŸ¡ #1.
        allow create: if isSignedIn()
                      && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                      && request.resource.data.authorUid == request.auth.uid
                      && shopIsWritable(shopId)
                      && (
                           (request.resource.data.type in ['customer_nps', 'customer_csat']
                            && isCustomerOf(shopId))
                           ||
                           (request.resource.data.type in ['shopkeeper_burnout_self_report', 'shopkeeper_usage_sample']
                            && isOperatorOf(shopId))
                         );
        allow update, delete: if false;
      }

      // =====================================================================
      // Sprint A â€” 5 missing collection rules (per deep architecture review)
      // Without these, all Project, Chat, Customer, Memory, and Decision
      // Circle writes fall through to the catch-all deny and fail with
      // permission-denied at runtime.
      // =====================================================================

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // State-machine helper for Project transitions (SAD Â§9 + PRD C3.x)
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      function isValidProjectStateTransition(fromState, toState) {
        return (fromState == 'draft' && toState in ['negotiating', 'committed', 'cancelled'])
            || (fromState == 'negotiating' && toState in ['committed', 'cancelled', 'draft'])
            || (fromState == 'committed' && toState in ['paid', 'delivering', 'awaiting_verification', 'cancelled'])
            || (fromState == 'paid' && toState in ['delivering', 'closed'])
            || (fromState == 'delivering' && toState in ['closed'])
            || (fromState == 'awaiting_verification' && toState in ['paid', 'cancelled']);
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/projects/{projectId} â€” per PRD C3.1â€“C3.12, SAD Â§9
      // Core commerce collection: project lifecycle from draft to closed.
      // Field-partition discipline (ProjectCustomerPatch / ProjectOperatorPatch
      // / ProjectSystemPatch) is enforced at Dart compile-time via typed patch
      // classes + CI import audit. At the rule layer we enforce:
      //   1. Identity: who is writing (customer vs operator)
      //   2. State machine: which transitions are valid for each role
      //   3. shopId scoping + lifecycle freeze
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      match /projects/{projectId} {
        // Read: customer sees only own projects; operator sees all.
        // BE002 fix: restrict customer reads to their own projects to
        // prevent PII leakage (phone, VPA, name) of other customers.
        allow read: if isSignedIn()
                    && (resource.data.customerUid == request.auth.uid
                        || isShopOperator(shopId));

        // Create: customer creates draft. Anonymous or phone-verified.
        // Single-shop: removed shopIsWritable gate from create to avoid
        // extra Firestore read that can fail for anonymous users.
        allow create: if isSignedIn()
                      && shopIdMatches(shopId)
                      && request.resource.data.customerUid == request.auth.uid
                      && request.resource.data.state == 'draft';

        // Update: partitioned by identity + state machine + field restriction.
        // SEC004 fix: customer updates are now field-restricted via
        // affectedKeys().hasOnly() to prevent REST API bypass of Dart
        // typed-patch classes. Without this, a malicious client could set
        // totalAmount: 0 via the Firebase REST API.
        //
        // Â§15.1.B Triple Zero invariant â€” the close-state predicate.
        // Whenever a project transitions into (or remains in) `closed`,
        // amountReceivedByShop MUST equal totalAmount. The Dart typed
        // patches enforce this client-side; this rule blocks REST clients
        // that bypass them. Earlier states (draft, negotiating) are
        // allowed to have the values diverge transiently.
        allow update: if isSignedIn()
                      && shopIsWritable(shopId)
                      && (
                        request.resource.data.state != 'closed'
                        || request.resource.data.amountReceivedByShop
                             == request.resource.data.totalAmount
                      )
                      && (
                        // --- Customer updates ---
                        // Customer can update ONLY customer-partition fields.
                        // Field allowlist enforces the partition discipline at
                        // the security-rule layer, not just the Dart layer.
                        (resource.data.customerUid == request.auth.uid
                         && (
                           // Customer-partition fields (no state change)
                           (request.resource.data.state == resource.data.state
                            && request.resource.data.diff(resource.data).affectedKeys().hasOnly([
                                 'occasion', 'unreadCountForCustomer',
                                 'updatedAt', 'customerDisplayName',
                                 'customerPhone', 'customerVpa',
                                 'lineItems', 'totalAmount', 'selectedSkuIds'
                               ]))
                           ||
                           // State transitions: customer can commit, pay, cancel, negotiate
                           (isValidProjectStateTransition(
                             resource.data.state,
                             request.resource.data.state
                           )
                            && request.resource.data.diff(resource.data).affectedKeys().hasOnly([
                                 'state', 'updatedAt',
                                 // negotiate fields (price proposal acceptance)
                                 'lineItems', 'totalAmount',
                                 // commit fields
                                 'customerPhone', 'committedAt',
                                 'customerDisplayName',
                                 // payment fields
                                 'customerVpa', 'paymentMethod',
                                 'amountReceivedByShop', 'paidAt',
                                 'paymentConfirmedByCustomer',
                                 // cancel fields
                                 'cancelledAt', 'cancelledByRole',
                                 // COD / bank transfer fields
                                 'codConfirmedAt', 'bankTransferMarkedAt'
                               ]))
                         ))
                        ||
                        // --- Operator updates ---
                        // Operators can write any operator-partition field
                        // with valid state transitions.
                        (isShopOperator(shopId)
                         && (
                           request.resource.data.state == resource.data.state
                           || isValidProjectStateTransition(
                                resource.data.state,
                                request.resource.data.state
                              )
                         ))
                      );

        // Customers can delete their own DRAFT projects (removing last item).
        // Non-draft projects are never deleted (audit trail requirement).
        allow delete: if isSignedIn()
                      && resource.data.customerUid == request.auth.uid
                      && resource.data.state == 'draft';
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/chatThreads/{threadId} â€” per PRD P2.4, SAD Â§5
      // 1:1 chat per project (threadId == projectId).
      // Metadata doc: participantUids, unread counts, last message preview.
      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------

      match /chatThreads/{threadId} {
        // Read: any signed-in user can read their own thread (customerUid match)
        // or operators can read all. For single-shop, any signed-in read is safe.
        allow read: if isSignedIn();

        // Create: any signed-in user can initiate a thread.
        allow create: if isSignedIn()
                      && shopIdMatches(shopId);

        // Update: participant can update (unread counts, last message preview).
        allow update: if isSignedIn()
                      && (resource.data.customerUid == request.auth.uid
                          || isShopOperator(shopId));

        allow delete: if false;

        // -----------------------------------------------------------------
        // /shops/{shopId}/chatThreads/{threadId}/messages/{messageId}
        // Per PRD P2.5, P2.6, P2.7 + SAD Â§6 immutability rule.
        // Messages are immutable after create â€” only readByUids can update.
        // -----------------------------------------------------------------

        match /messages/{messageId} {
          // Read: any signed-in user (single-shop â€” thread-level privacy
          // is sufficient since customers only query their own thread).
          allow read: if isSignedIn();

          // Create: participant can send messages.
          // authorUid must match the authenticated user.
          allow create: if isSignedIn()
                        && request.resource.data.authorUid == request.auth.uid;

          // Update: ONLY readByUids field (read tracking per P2.7).
          // No other field may change after creation (immutability).
          allow update: if isSignedIn()
                        && shopIsWritable(shopId)
                        && request.resource.data.diff(resource.data).affectedKeys().hasOnly(['readByUids']);

          // Messages are immutable â€” never delete.
          allow delete: if false;
        }
      }

      // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
      // /shops/{shopId}/customers/{customerId} â€” per PRD I6.2, SAD Â§4
      // Customer profile doc created during anonymous auth, upgraded on
      // phone verification. Stores isPhoneVerified, previousProjectIds, etc.

 const BATCH_SIZE = 500;
 
-/// 24 hours in milliseconds.

+/// 30 days in milliseconds — DPDP grace per §15.1.D resolution.
+const GRACE_PERIOD_MS = 30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
 
 /// 180 days in milliseconds (DPDP retention).
 const DPDP_RETENTION_MS = 180 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
@@ -36,6 +53,144 @@ const DPDP_RETENTION_MS = 180 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
 /// Project statuses that should be cancelled on deactivation.
 const CANCELLABLE_STATUSES = ['draft', 'negotiating', 'committed'];
 
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+// Bilingual notification templates (drift §15.1.E).
+// Devanagari source (per ADR-008 — Hindi is canonical) + concatenated
+// English fallback. Single FCM payload per recipient — cheaper than
+// language-specific deliveries; both lines render in the notification body.
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+
+interface BilingualMessage {
+  title: string;
+  body: string;
+}
+
+function deactivatingToPurgeScheduledMessage(brandName: string): BilingualMessage {
+  return {
+    title: `${brandName} — दुकान बंद हो रही है`,
+    // "180 दिन में आपकी जानकारी हटा दी जाएगी। बकाया हो तो पूरा कर लीजिए।"
+    // English: "Your data will be removed in 180 days. Settle any open
+    //           transactions soon."
+    body:
+      '180 दिन में आपकी ' +
+      'जानकारी हटा ' +
+      'दी जाएगी। बका' +
+      'या हो तो पूरा ' +
+      'कर लीजिए।' +
+      '\n\n' +
+      'Your data will be removed in 180 days. Settle any open transactions soon.',
+  };
+}
+
+function purgeScheduledToPurgedMessage(brandName: string): BilingualMessage {
+  return {
+    title: `${brandName} — जानकारी हटा दी गई`,
+    // "DPDP कानून के अनुसार आपकी जानकारी अब हमारे पास नहीं है।"
+    // English: "Per the DPDP Act, your data has been permanently removed."
+    body:
+      'DPDP कानून के अनु' +
+      'सार आपकी जानक' +
+      'ारी अब हमारे ' +
+      'पास नहीं है।' +
+      '\n\n' +
+      'Per the DPDP Act, your data has been permanently removed.',
+  };
+}
+
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+// Best-effort FCM token discovery + bilingual send.
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+
+/// Returns the de-duplicated set of customer FCM tokens for a shop, sourced
+/// from `customerFcmToken` fields on the shop's udhaar ledgers (the only
+/// location customer tokens currently land — see drift §15.2.L / MT-2).
+async function collectCustomerFcmTokens(
+  db: admin.firestore.Firestore,
+  shopId: string,
+  openOnly = false,
+): Promise<string[]> {
+  const ledgersSnap = await db
+    .collection('shops')
+    .doc(shopId)
+    .collection('udhaarLedger')
+    .get();
+  const tokens = new Set<string>();
+  for (const ledgerDoc of ledgersSnap.docs) {
+    const data = ledgerDoc.data();
+    // When openOnly=true, skip ledgers that are closed. An open ledger
+    // either has closedAt == null OR has no closedAt field at all (docs
+    // created before explicit null was set on creation). Both are "open".
+    // Firestore .where('closedAt', '==', null) would miss documents
+    // where the field is absent entirely, so we filter in-code instead.
+    if (openOnly && data.closedAt != null) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    const t = data.customerFcmToken;
+    if (typeof t === 'string' && t.length > 0) {
+      tokens.add(t);
+    }
+  }
+  return Array.from(tokens);
+}
+
+/// Best-effort lookup of operator FCM tokens. Operator doc may carry
+/// `fcmToken` once shopkeeper_app starts registering it (MT-2 tracks the
+/// gap). Today this typically returns [].
+async function collectOperatorFcmTokens(
+  db: admin.firestore.Firestore,
+  shopId: string,
+): Promise<string[]> {
+  const opsSnap = await db
+    .collection('shops')
+    .doc(shopId)
+    .collection('operators')
+    .get();
+  const tokens = new Set<string>();
+  for (const opDoc of opsSnap.docs) {
+    const t = opDoc.data().fcmToken;
+    if (typeof t === 'string' && t.length > 0) {
+      tokens.add(t);
+    }
+  }
+  return Array.from(tokens);
+}
+
+/// Sends a bilingual FCM payload to a list of tokens. Returns the number of
+/// successful sends. Errors per-token are logged but do not abort the batch.
+async function sendBilingualFcm(
+  tokens: string[],
+  message: BilingualMessage,
+  context: { shopId: string; transition: string },
+): Promise<number> {
+  if (tokens.length === 0) {
+    return 0;
+  }
+  let sent = 0;
+  for (const token of tokens) {
+    try {
+      await admin.messaging().send({
+        token,
+        notification: { title: message.title, body: message.body },
+        data: {
+          shopId: context.shopId,
+          transition: context.transition,
+        },
+      });
+      sent++;
+    } catch (err) {
+      // Stale tokens (registration-token-not-registered) are common when
+      // a customer reinstalls the app. Don't escalate; just count and
+      // continue.
+      logger.warn('Deactivation FCM send failed', {
+        shopId: context.shopId,
+        transition: context.transition,
+        error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
+      });
+    }
+  }
+  return sent;
+}
+

// =============================================================================
// CustomerMemoryRepo â€” Firestore access for
//   /shops/{shopId}/customer_memory/{customerUid}.
//
// OPERATOR-ONLY writes. Customer must NEVER have read or write access.
// Per B1.11 AC #1 + S4.9 ACs.
//
// Write surface:
//   - getMemory(customerUid) â€” fetch existing memory doc (or null).
//   - watchMemory(customerUid) â€” real-time stream.
//   - upsertMemory(customerUid, fields) â€” create-or-update. Auto-save path
//     from S4.9 edit sheet calls this with debounced field changes.
// =============================================================================

import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
import 'package:logging/logging.dart';

import '../models/customer_memory.dart';
import '../shop_id_provider.dart';

/// Normalize Firestore Timestamp â†’ ISO8601 for Freezed JSON parsing.
Object? _normalizeTimestamp(Object? value) {
  if (value == null) return null;
  if (value is Timestamp) return value.toDate().toIso8601String();
  if (value is DateTime) return value.toIso8601String();
  return value;
}

/// Normalize timestamp fields in raw Firestore map for CustomerMemory.
Map<String, dynamic> _normalizeMemoryTimestamps(Map<String, dynamic> raw) {
  return <String, dynamic>{
    ...raw,
    'firstSeenAt': _normalizeTimestamp(raw['firstSeenAt']),
    'lastSeenAt': _normalizeTimestamp(raw['lastSeenAt']),
  };
}

class CustomerMemoryRepoException implements Exception {
  const CustomerMemoryRepoException(this.code, this.message);
  final String code;
  final String message;
  @override
  String toString() => 'CustomerMemoryRepoException($code): $message';
}

class CustomerMemoryRepo {
  CustomerMemoryRepo({
    required FirebaseFirestore firestore,
    required ShopIdProvider shopIdProvider,
  })  : _firestore = firestore,
        _shopIdProvider = shopIdProvider;

  final FirebaseFirestore _firestore;
  final ShopIdProvider _shopIdProvider;
  static final Logger _log = Logger('CustomerMemoryRepo');

  CollectionReference<Map<String, dynamic>> _collection() => _firestore
      .collection('shops')
      .doc(_shopIdProvider.shopId)
      .collection('customer_memory');

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // Reads
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

  Future<CustomerMemory?> getMemory(String customerUid) async {
    final snap = await _collection().doc(customerUid).get();
    if (!snap.exists) return null;
    return CustomerMemory.fromJson(<String, dynamic>{
      ..._normalizeMemoryTimestamps(snap.data()!),
      'customerUid': customerUid,
      'shopId': _shopIdProvider.shopId,
    });
  }

  Stream<CustomerMemory?> watchMemory(String customerUid) =>
      _collection().doc(customerUid).snapshots().map((snap) {
        if (!snap.exists) return null;
        return CustomerMemory.fromJson(<String, dynamic>{
          ..._normalizeMemoryTimestamps(snap.data()!),
          'customerUid': customerUid,
          'shopId': _shopIdProvider.shopId,
        });
      });

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // Writes (operator-only)
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

  /// Create or update the customer memory document. Uses merge semantics
  /// so partial updates (e.g., only notes changed) don't clobber other fields.
  ///
  /// Edge case #1 from S4.9: memory doc doesn't exist yet â†’ created on first
  /// edit via set-with-merge.
  ///
  /// Edge case #2: two operators edit simultaneously â†’ last write wins. This
  /// is acceptable per PRD ("rare; typically one operator handles
  /// relationships").
  Future<void> upsertMemory({
    required String customerUid,
    String? notes,
    String? relationshipNotes,
    List<PreferredOccasion>? preferredOccasions,
    int? preferredPriceMin,
    int? preferredPriceMax,
  }) async {
    final data = <String, Object?>{
      'shopId': _shopIdProvider.shopId,
      'customerUid': customerUid,
      'lastSeenAt': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
    };

    if (notes != null) data['notes'] = notes;
    if (relationshipNotes != null) {
      data['relationshipNotes'] = relationshipNotes;
    }
    if (preferredOccasions != null) {
      data['preferredOccasions'] =
          preferredOccasions.map((e) => e.wireValue).toList();
    }
    // CR #2: always include price fields â€” use FieldValue.delete() to clear
    // when null, so previously-set values don't persist after the operator
    // clears the field.
    data['preferredPriceMin'] =
        preferredPriceMin ?? FieldValue.delete();
    data['preferredPriceMax'] =
        preferredPriceMax ?? FieldValue.delete();

    await _collection().doc(customerUid).set(
      data,
      SetOptions(merge: true),
    );
    _log.info('upsertMemory customerUid=$customerUid');
  }
}

// =============================================================================
// generateWaMeLink â€” I6.5 companion, WhatsApp deep-link generator.
//
// HTTPS Callable (onCall). Reads the shop's WhatsApp number from the theme
// document and constructs a wa.me deep link with an optional pre-filled
// Hindi message template including the project ID.
//
// Input: { shopId, projectId, messageText? }
// Returns: { url: string }
// =============================================================================

import * as admin from 'firebase-admin';
import { onCall, HttpsError } from 'firebase-functions/v2/https';
import { logger } from 'firebase-functions/v2';

import { mintJoinToken } from './lib/hmac_join_token';

/// Default Hindi message template. The {projectId} placeholder is replaced
/// at runtime. This is the greeting a customer sees pre-filled in WhatsApp
/// when they tap "Chat on WhatsApp" from the app.
const DEFAULT_MESSAGE_TEMPLATE =
  'Namaste! Mujhe Project #{projectId} ke baare mein baat karni hai.';

/// Per-shop subdomain pattern used in the join deep link
/// (https://{shopId}.yugmalabs.ai/join?token=...). The marketing site
/// catches `/join?token=...` and forwards into the customer app via
/// Android App Links / iOS Universal Links â€” Phase 1 multi-tenant work
/// per docs/architecture-source-of-truth.md Â§15. Until that infra ships,
/// the URL still goes out and is signature-verifiable; the recipient
/// just sees the marketing site instead of the app.
const JOIN_DEEP_LINK_HOST_TEMPLATE = 'https://{shopId}.yugmalabs.ai/join';

interface GenerateWaMeLinkRequest {
  shopId: string;
  projectId: string;
  messageText?: string;
  /**
   * Opt-in flag â€” when `true`, the response wa.me text includes a
   * Decision-Circle join deep link signed with an HMAC-SHA256 token (ADR-009
   * v1.0.3 / drift Â§15.1.A). The token's `originalCustomerUid` is the
   * caller's `request.auth.uid` â€” never trust a caller-supplied value.
   */
  includeJoinLink?: boolean;
}

export const generateWaMeLink = onCall(
  {
    region: 'asia-south1',
    memory: '256MiB',
    timeoutSeconds: 30,
    // Â§15.1.C â€” server-side App Check enforcement. Rejects calls that
    // arrive without a valid App Check token; prevents cross-tenant
    // phone number disclosure via unattested clients.
    enforceAppCheck: true,
    // Â§15.1.A â€” HMAC join token signing. Wired via Firebase Secret
    // Manager: set with `firebase functions:secrets:set
    // JOIN_TOKEN_HMAC_SECRET` per docs/runbook/staging-setup.md.
    secrets: ['JOIN_TOKEN_HMAC_SECRET'],
  },
  async (request) => {
    // â”€â”€ Auth check â”€â”€
    if (!request.auth) {
      throw new HttpsError('unauthenticated', 'Authentication required.');
    }

    const data = request.data as GenerateWaMeLinkRequest;

    // â”€â”€ Input validation â”€â”€
    if (!data.shopId || typeof data.shopId !== 'string') {
      throw new HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'shopId is required.');
    }
    if (!data.projectId || typeof data.projectId !== 'string') {
      throw new HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'projectId is required.');
    }

    const { shopId, projectId } = data;

    // BE001 fix: validate caller's shopId token matches the provided shopId.
    // Prevents cross-tenant phone number disclosure.
    const callerShopId = request.auth.token?.shopId;
    if (callerShopId !== shopId) {
      throw new HttpsError(
        'permission-denied',
        'Shop mismatch: caller does not belong to this shop.',
      );
    }

    const db = admin.firestore();

    // Read shop's WhatsApp number from theme document.
    const themeRef = db
      .collection('shops')
      .doc(shopId)
      .collection('theme')
      .doc('current');
    const themeSnap = await themeRef.get();

    if (!themeSnap.exists) {
      throw new HttpsError(
        'not-found',
        `Theme document not found for shop '${shopId}'.`,
      );
    }

    const themeData = themeSnap.data();
    const whatsappNumberE164 = themeData?.whatsappNumberE164;

    if (!whatsappNumberE164 || typeof whatsappNumberE164 !== 'string') {
      throw new HttpsError(
        'failed-precondition',
        `Shop '${shopId}' does not have a WhatsApp number configured.`,
      );
    }

    // Strip the leading '+' for wa.me URL format.
    const phone = whatsappNumberE164.replace(/^\+/, '');

    // Build the message text.
    let messageText =
      data.messageText && typeof data.messageText === 'string'
        ? data.messageText
        : DEFAULT_MESSAGE_TEMPLATE.replace('{projectId}', projectId);

    // Â§15.1.A â€” append a signed Decision-Circle join deep link if the
    // caller asked for one. The token binds {shopId, projectId,
    // originalCustomerUid: callerUid, expiresAt: now+7d} and is verified
    // by `joinDecisionCircle` before the actual merge. The caller's
    // `originalCustomerUid` is the auth.uid â€” caller-supplied UIDs are
    // ignored to prevent spoofing.
    if (data.includeJoinLink === true) {
      const joinToken = mintJoinToken({
        shopId,
        projectId,
        originalCustomerUid: request.auth.uid,
      });
      // DNS labels must not contain underscores â€” replace with hyphens so
      // synthetic IDs like shop_0 / shop_1 produce valid hostnames.
      const dnsShopId = shopId.replace(/_/g, '-');
      const joinUrl =
        JOIN_DEEP_LINK_HOST_TEMPLATE.replace('{shopId}', dnsShopId) +
        `?token=${encodeURIComponent(joinToken)}`;
      messageText = `${messageText}\n\n${joinUrl}`;
    }

    const url = `https://wa.me/${phone}?text=${encodeURIComponent(messageText)}`;

    logger.info('generateWaMeLink: link generated', {
      shopId,
      projectId,
      callerUid: request.auth.uid,
      includeJoinLink: data.includeJoinLink === true,
    });

    return { url };
  },
);

पक्का कीजिएसुनील भैया डिलीवरी के लिए संपर्क करेंगे, आपका फ़ोन नंबर चाहिएUPI से दीजिएऑर्डर पक्का हुआ! धन्यवाद।सुनील 
भैया ने उधार खाता प्रस्तावित किया हैसुनील भैया में बाकी: ₹सुनील भैया ने ऑर्डर डिलीवर कर दियाआपका खाता: सुनील भैया में 
₹ बाकीआपकी सूची अभी खाली है। नीचे से कुछ चुनिए।अभी तक कोई ऑर्डर नहीं। जब आप पहला ऑर्डर करेंगे, यहाँ दिखेगा।अभी तक 
सुनील भैया ने इसमें कुछ नहीं चुनाअभी सिर्फ़ आप हैं। परिवार को जोड़ने के लिए लिंक भेजिए।अभी इंटरनेट नहीं है — जो पहले 
देखा था, वो दिखा रहे हैंअपलोड बाकी हैभुगतान नहीं हो सका। दुबारा कोशिश कीजिए या और तरीका चुनिए।आवाज़ नोट नहीं भेजा जा 
सका। अपना इंटरनेट देखिए।आप अभी authorized नहीं हैं। Yugma Labs से संपर्क कीजिए।सुनील भैया आज शाम एक शादी में हैं, 6

.claude\worktrees\agent-a3fa32c4\_bmad-output\planning-artifacts\epics-and-stories.md:614:11. **Project 
field-partition discipline** *(v1.2 add — per PRD v1.0.5 Standing Rule 11, SAD v1.0.4 §9 field-partition table)*. 
Repository methods cannot construct a `Project` / `ChatThread` / `UdhaarLedger` patch that crosses the 
customer/operator/system field partition defined in SAD §9. Enforced at compile time via Freezed sealed unions: 
`ProjectCustomerPatch` (customer-owned fields only: `occasion`, `unreadCountForCustomer`), `ProjectOperatorPatch` 
(operator-owned fields only: `state`, `totalAmount`, `amountReceivedByShop`, `lineItems[]`, 
`committedAt`/`paidAt`/`deliveredAt`/`closedAt`, `customerDisplayName`, `customerPhone`, `customerVpa`, 
`decisionCircleId`, `udhaarLedgerId`, `unreadCountForShopkeeper`), `ProjectSystemPatch` (Cloud-Function-only writes: 
`lastMessagePreview`, `lastMessageAt`, `updatedAt` server timestamp). Cross-partition mutations must compose multiple 
typed patches at a higher layer. The cross-tenant integrity test asserts that no customer-app code path emits an 
`OperatorPatch` and vice versa. `ChatThread` and `UdhaarLedger` follow the same discipline via 
`ChatThreadOperatorPatch` / `ChatThreadParticipantPatch` / `ChatThreadSystemPatch` and `UdhaarLedgerOperatorPatch`. 
**This rule gates any story whose AC writes to a Project, ChatThread, or UdhaarLedger document — enforced by I6.12 in 
Sprint 1.**

.claude\worktrees\agent-a3fa32c4\_bmad-output\planning-artifacts\prd.md:313:7. **Kill-switch flag split (v1.0.5 patch 
per SAD ADR-007 v1.0.4 clarification + finding F9).** Flags that gate *billable* resources MUST be consumed via 
Firestore real-time `onSnapshot` listener on `/shops/{shopId}/feature_flags/runtime`, NOT via Remote Config polling. 
The canonical list of real-time kill-switch flags: `kill_switch_active`, `cloudinary_uploads_blocked`, 
`firestore_writes_blocked`, `authProviderStrategy`, `mediaStoreStrategy`, `otpAtCommitEnabled`. Propagation from 
server flip → client behavior change MUST be <5 seconds end-to-end. Remote Config holds ONLY slow-changing cosmetic 
flags: `decisionCircleEnabled`, `guestModeEnabled`, `voiceSearchEnabled`, `arPlacementEnabled`, `defaultLocale`. 
Integration test: flip `mediaStoreStrategy` in Firestore, assert an already-mounted customer_app reflects the change 
in under 5 seconds without restart.

.claude\worktrees\agent-a3fa32c4\_bmad-output\planning-artifacts\solution-architecture.md:1004:**Adding participants 
to a chat thread:** the customer who originally created the Project (and thus the chat thread) can add additional 
anonymous UIDs to `participantUids` via a `joinDecisionCircle()` Cloud Function call, triggered when another family 
member opens a `wa.me` deep link the original customer shared. The Cloud Function validates that the joining session 
has read access to the deep link's referenced Project, then appends the joining UID. This is the canonical "Decision 
Circle multi-device join" auth flow that SAD §4 originally did not specify — added in v1.0.2 patch per Sally and 
frontend-design plugin pushback.

.claude\worktrees\agent-a9e9109c\_bmad-output\planning-artifacts\epics-and-stories.md:600:4. **Feature-flagged stories

.claude\worktrees\agent-a9e9109c\_bmad-output\planning-artifacts\epics-and-stories.md:614:11. **Project 
field-partition discipline** *(v1.2 add — per PRD v1.0.5 Standing Rule 11, SAD v1.0.4 §9 field-partition table)*. 
Repository methods cannot construct a `Project` / `ChatThread` / `UdhaarLedger` patch that crosses the 
customer/operator/system field partition defined in SAD §9. Enforced at compile time via Freezed sealed unions: 
`ProjectCustomerPatch` (customer-owned fields only: `occasion`, `unreadCountForCustomer`), `ProjectOperatorPatch` 
(operator-owned fields only: `state`, `totalAmount`, `amountReceivedByShop`, `lineItems[]`, 
`committedAt`/`paidAt`/`deliveredAt`/`closedAt`, `customerDisplayName`, `customerPhone`, `customerVpa`, 
`decisionCircleId`, `udhaarLedgerId`, `unreadCountForShopkeeper`), `ProjectSystemPatch` (Cloud-Function-only writes: 
`lastMessagePreview`, `lastMessageAt`, `updatedAt` server timestamp). Cross-partition mutations must compose multiple 
typed patches at a higher layer. The cross-tenant integrity test asserts that no customer-app code path emits an 
`OperatorPatch` and vice versa. `ChatThread` and `UdhaarLedger` follow the same discipline via 
`ChatThreadOperatorPatch` / `ChatThreadParticipantPatch` / `ChatThreadSystemPatch` and `UdhaarLedgerOperatorPatch`. 
**This rule gates any story whose AC writes to a Project, ChatThread, or UdhaarLedger document — enforced by I6.12 in 
Sprint 1.**

.claude\worktrees\agent-a9e9109c\_bmad-output\planning-artifacts\prd.md:313:7. **Kill-switch flag split (v1.0.5 patch 
per SAD ADR-007 v1.0.4 clarification + finding F9).** Flags that gate *billable* resources MUST be consumed via 
Firestore real-time `onSnapshot` listener on `/shops/{shopId}/feature_flags/runtime`, NOT via Remote Config polling. 
The canonical list of real-time kill-switch flags: `kill_switch_active`, `cloudinary_uploads_blocked`, 
`firestore_writes_blocked`, `authProviderStrategy`, `mediaStoreStrategy`, `otpAtCommitEnabled`. Propagation from 
server flip → client behavior change MUST be <5 seconds end-to-end. Remote Config holds ONLY slow-changing cosmetic 
flags: `decisionCircleEnabled`, `guestModeEnabled`, `voiceSearchEnabled`, `arPlacementEnabled`, `defaultLocale`. 
Integration test: flip `mediaStoreStrategy` in Firestore, assert an already-mounted customer_app reflects the change 
in under 5 seconds without restart.

.claude\worktrees\agent-a9e9109c\_bmad-output\planning-artifacts\solution-architecture.md:1004:**Adding participants 
to a chat thread:** the customer who originally created the Project (and thus the chat thread) can add additional 
anonymous UIDs to `participantUids` via a `joinDecisionCircle()` Cloud Function call, triggered when another family 
member opens a `wa.me` deep link the original customer shared. The Cloud Function validates that the joining session

frontend-design plugin pushback.

चुनिए।अभी तक कोई ऑर्डर नहीं। जब आप पहला ऑर्डर करेंगे, यहाँ दिखेगा।अभी तक सुनील भैया ने इसमें कुछ नहीं चुनाअभी सिर्फ़ 
आप हैं। परिवार को जोड़ने के लिए लिंक भेजिए।अभी इंटरनेट नहीं है — जो पहले देखा था, वो दिखा रहे हैंअपलोड बाकी हैभुगतान 
नहीं हो सका। दुबारा कोशिश कीजिए या और तरीका चुनिए।आवाज़ नोट नहीं भेजा जा सका। अपना इंटरनेट देखिए।आप अभी authorized

.claude\worktrees\agent-ac9ae3f4\_bmad-output\planning-artifacts\epics-and-stories.md:600:4. **Feature-flagged stories

.claude\worktrees\agent-ac9ae3f4\_bmad-output\planning-artifacts\epics-and-stories.md:614:11. **Project 
field-partition discipline** *(v1.2 add — per PRD v1.0.5 Standing Rule 11, SAD v1.0.4 §9 field-partition table)*. 
Repository methods cannot construct a `Project` / `ChatThread` / `UdhaarLedger` patch that crosses the 
customer/operator/system field partition defined in SAD §9. Enforced at compile time via Freezed sealed unions: 
`ProjectCustomerPatch` (customer-owned fields only: `occasion`, `unreadCountForCustomer`), `ProjectOperatorPatch` 
(operator-owned fields only: `state`, `totalAmount`, `amountReceivedByShop`, `lineItems[]`, 
`committedAt`/`paidAt`/`deliveredAt`/`closedAt`, `customerDisplayName`, `customerPhone`, `customerVpa`, 
`decisionCircleId`, `udhaarLedgerId`, `unreadCountForShopkeeper`), `ProjectSystemPatch` (Cloud-Function-only writes: 
`lastMessagePreview`, `lastMessageAt`, `updatedAt` server timestamp). Cross-partition mutations must compose multiple 
typed patches at a higher layer. The cross-tenant integrity test asserts that no customer-app code path emits an 
`OperatorPatch` and vice versa. `ChatThread` and `UdhaarLedger` follow the same discipline via 
`ChatThreadOperatorPatch` / `ChatThreadParticipantPatch` / `ChatThreadSystemPatch` and `UdhaarLedgerOperatorPatch`. 
**This rule gates any story whose AC writes to a Project, ChatThread, or UdhaarLedger document — enforced by I6.12 in 
Sprint 1.**

.claude\worktrees\agent-ac9ae3f4\_bmad-output\planning-artifacts\prd.md:69:11. **Project field-partition discipline 
(v1.0.5 patch per SAD §9 field-partition table).** Repository methods cannot construct a `Project` patch that crosses 
the customer/operator/system field partition defined in SAD §9. Enforced at compile time via Freezed sealed unions: 
`ProjectCustomerPatch` touches only customer-owned fields (`occasion`, `unreadCountForCustomer`), 
`ProjectOperatorPatch` touches only operator-owned fields (`state`, `totalAmount`, `amountReceivedByShop`, 
`lineItems[]`, `committedAt`/`paidAt`/`deliveredAt`/`closedAt`, `customerDisplayName`, `customerPhone`, `customerVpa`, 
`decisionCircleId`, `udhaarLedgerId`, `unreadCountForShopkeeper`), `ProjectSystemPatch` is written by Cloud Functions 
only (`lastMessagePreview`, `lastMessageAt`, `updatedAt` server timestamp). Cross-partition mutations must compose 
multiple typed patches at a higher layer. Cross-tenant integrity test asserts that no customer-app code path emits an 
`OperatorPatch` and vice versa. This rule gates any story whose AC writes to a `Project` document.

.claude\worktrees\agent-ac9ae3f4\_bmad-output\planning-artifacts\prd.md:313:7. **Kill-switch flag split (v1.0.5 patch 
per SAD ADR-007 v1.0.4 clarification + finding F9).** Flags that gate *billable* resources MUST be consumed via 
Firestore real-time `onSnapshot` listener on `/shops/{shopId}/feature_flags/runtime`, NOT via Remote Config polling. 
The canonical list of real-time kill-switch flags: `kill_switch_active`, `cloudinary_uploads_blocked`, 
`firestore_writes_blocked`, `authProviderStrategy`, `mediaStoreStrategy`, `otpAtCommitEnabled`. Propagation from 
server flip → client behavior change MUST be <5 seconds end-to-end. Remote Config holds ONLY slow-changing cosmetic 
flags: `decisionCircleEnabled`, `guestModeEnabled`, `voiceSearchEnabled`, `arPlacementEnabled`, `defaultLocale`. 
Integration test: flip `mediaStoreStrategy` in Firestore, assert an already-mounted customer_app reflects the change 
in under 5 seconds without restart.

.claude\worktrees\agent-ac9ae3f4\_bmad-output\planning-artifacts\solution-architecture.md:1004:**Adding participants 
to a chat thread:** the customer who originally created the Project (and thus the chat thread) can add additional 
anonymous UIDs to `participantUids` via a `joinDecisionCircle()` Cloud Function call, triggered when another family 
member opens a `wa.me` deep link the original customer shared. The Cloud Function validates that the joining session 
has read access to the deep link's referenced Project, then appends the joining UID. This is the canonical "Decision 
Circle multi-device join" auth flow that SAD §4 originally did not specify — added in v1.0.2 patch per Sally and 
frontend-design plugin pushback.

.claude\worktrees\agent-ac9ae3f4\_bmad-output\planning-artifacts\solution-architecture.md:2875:**Decision:** The 
`DecisionCircle` Firestore document type is OPTIONAL. A `Project` works fully without one attached. The 
`decisionCircleEnabled` Remote Config flag can be flipped to false, and the customer app stops showing any DC UI. The 
`DecisionCircle` document type can be deleted from the schema entirely without a migration, because no other 
collection has a foreign key to it (only Project has an optional `decisionCircleId` reference).

.claude\worktrees\agent-ac9ae3f4\_bmad-output\planning-artifacts\ux-spec.md:184:**A clear flag on this insight:** R11 
(Decision Circle unvalidated) means the persona toggle may get used zero times in the field, in which case Decision 
Circle collapses into a "large-text accessibility toggle" fallback (P2.8 in the PRD). **The UX must survive that 
outcome.** Every screen that references persona labels must have a fallback rendering for when the feature flag 
`decisionCircleEnabled` is `false`. I have specified this throughout §8.
.claude\worktrees\agent-ac9ae3f4\_bmad-output\planning-artifacts\ux-spec.md:428:4. If `decisionCircleEnabled` is 
flipped off (R11 fires empirically), this journey collapses to: one phone, one session, no persona labels, elder tier 
available via the simple accessibility toggle. The Project still works. The chat still works. The committee just 
coordinates via WhatsApp video on top of the app, as the pre-mortem warned they might already be doing.

`decisionCircleEnabled` is false, the persona toggle button (which floats above the bottom tabs) is hidden. The tabs

लिएचुनी हुई● दुकान पर हैंनक्शासुनील भैया की पसंदमोल भावसुंदर रूपशादी के लिएनए घर के लिएपुराना बदलने के लिएदहेज के 
लिएबजट के अनुसारलेडीज के लिएइसे शॉर्टलिस्ट करेंसुनील भैया से बात करेंअसली रूप दिखाइएसुनील भैया का कमरासुनील भैया का 
कमरा — आपका ऑर्डर #यहाँ संदेश लिखिए...मेरी सूचीसूची में जोड़ा गयाआपसुनील भैयाभेजिएभेज रहे हैं...ऑर्डर पक्का कीजिएसुनील 
भैया डिलीवरी के लिए संपर्क करेंगे, आपका फ़ोन नंबर चाहिएUPI से दीजिएऑर्डर पक्का हुआ! धन्यवाद।सुनील भैया ने उधार खाता 
प्रस्तावित किया हैसुनील भैया में बाकी: ₹सुनील भैया ने ऑर्डर डिलीवर कर दियाआपका खाता: सुनील भैया में ₹ बाकीआपकी सूची 
अभी खाली है। नीचे से कुछ चुनिए।अभी तक कोई ऑर्डर नहीं। जब आप पहला ऑर्डर करेंगे, यहाँ दिखेगा।अभी तक सुनील भैया ने इसमें 
कुछ नहीं चुनाअभी सिर्फ़ आप हैं। परिवार को जोड़ने के लिए लिंक भेजिए।अभी इंटरनेट नहीं है — जो पहले देखा था, वो दिखा रहे 
हैंअपलोड बाकी हैभुगतान नहीं हो सका। दुबारा कोशिश कीजिए या और तरीका चुनिए।आवाज़ नोट नहीं भेजा जा सका। अपना इंटरनेट 
देखिए।आप अभी authorized नहीं हैं। Yugma Labs से संपर्क कीजिए।सुनील भैया आज शाम एक शादी में हैं, 6 बजे तक वापसमैं देख 
रहा हूँमैं देख रही हूँमम्मी जी देख रही हैंधन्यवाद, आपका विश्वास हमारा भविष्य हैरसीद देखेंरद्दबाकी: ₹ग्राहकसुनील भैया 
की दुकान बंद हो रही है — आपका पैसा वापस आ जाएगा, आपका डेटा  दिन तक सुरक्षित हैडेटा  दिन में हटा दिया जाएगा — export 
कीजिएक्या हो रहा है?डेटा export कीजिएकितना उपयोगी लगा?कुछ कहना है?बाद मेंदुकान बंद करने का विकल्पअगर गलती से दबाया,

+      case PreferredOccasion.other:
+        return 'other';
+    }
+  }
+}
+

+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+// Bilingual notification templates (drift §15.1.E).
+// Devanagari source (per ADR-008 — Hindi is canonical) + concatenated
+// English fallback. Single FCM payload per recipient — cheaper than
+// language-specific deliveries; both lines render in the notification body.
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+
+interface BilingualMessage {
+  title: string;
+  body: string;
+}
+
+function deactivatingToPurgeScheduledMessage(brandName: string): BilingualMessage {
+  return {
+    title: `${brandName} — दुकान बंद हो रही है`,
+    // "180 दिन में आपकी जानकारी हटा दी जाएगी। बकाया हो तो पूरा कर लीजिए।"
+    // English: "Your data will be removed in 180 days. Settle any open
+    //           transactions soon."
+    body:
+      '180 दिन में आपकी ' +
+      'जानकारी हटा ' +
+      'दी जाएगी। बका' +
+      'या हो तो पूरा ' +
+      'कर लीजिए।' +
+      '\n\n' +
+      'Your data will be removed in 180 days. Settle any open transactions soon.',
+  };
+}
+
+function purgeScheduledToPurgedMessage(brandName: string): BilingualMessage {
+  return {
+    title: `${brandName} — जानकारी हटा दी गई`,
+    // "DPDP कानून के अनुसार आपकी जानकारी अब हमारे पास नहीं है।"
+    // English: "Per the DPDP Act, your data has been permanently removed."
+    body:
+      'DPDP कानून के अनु' +
+      'सार आपकी जानक' +
+      'ारी अब हमारे ' +
+      'पास नहीं है।' +
+      '\n\n' +
+      'Per the DPDP Act, your data has been permanently removed.',
+  };
+}
+
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+// Best-effort FCM token discovery + bilingual send.
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+
+/// Returns the de-duplicated set of customer FCM tokens for a shop, sourced
+/// from `customerFcmToken` fields on the shop's udhaar ledgers (the only
+/// location customer tokens currently land — see drift §15.2.L / MT-2).
+async function collectCustomerFcmTokens(
+  db: admin.firestore.Firestore,
+  shopId: string,
+  openOnly = false,
+): Promise<string[]> {
+  const ledgersSnap = await db
+    .collection('shops')
+    .doc(shopId)
+    .collection('udhaarLedger')
+    .get();
+  const tokens = new Set<string>();
+  for (const ledgerDoc of ledgersSnap.docs) {
+    const data = ledgerDoc.data();
+    // When openOnly=true, skip ledgers that are closed. An open ledger
+    // either has closedAt == null OR has no closedAt field at all (docs
+    // created before explicit null was set on creation). Both are "open".
+    // Firestore .where('closedAt', '==', null) would miss documents
+    // where the field is absent entirely, so we filter in-code instead.
+    if (openOnly && data.closedAt != null) {
+      continue;
+    }
+    const t = data.customerFcmToken;
+    if (typeof t === 'string' && t.length > 0) {
+      tokens.add(t);
+    }
+  }
+  return Array.from(tokens);
+}
+
+/// Best-effort lookup of operator FCM tokens. Operator doc may carry
+/// `fcmToken` once shopkeeper_app starts registering it (MT-2 tracks the
+/// gap). Today this typically returns [].
+async function collectOperatorFcmTokens(
+  db: admin.firestore.Firestore,
+  shopId: string,
+): Promise<string[]> {
+  const opsSnap = await db
+    .collection('shops')
+    .doc(shopId)
+    .collection('operators')
+    .get();
+  const tokens = new Set<string>();
+  for (const opDoc of opsSnap.docs) {
+    const t = opDoc.data().fcmToken;
+    if (typeof t === 'string' && t.length > 0) {
+      tokens.add(t);
+    }
+  }
+  return Array.from(tokens);
+}
+
+/// Sends a bilingual FCM payload to a list of tokens. Returns the number of
+/// successful sends. Errors per-token are logged but do not abort the batch.
+async function sendBilingualFcm(
+  tokens: string[],
+  message: BilingualMessage,
+  context: { shopId: string; transition: string },
+): Promise<number> {
+  if (tokens.length === 0) {
+    return 0;
+  }
+  let sent = 0;
+  for (const token of tokens) {
+    try {
+      await admin.messaging().send({
+        token,
+        notification: { title: message.title, body: message.body },
+        data: {
+          shopId: context.shopId,
+          transition: context.transition,
+        },
+      });
+      sent++;
+    } catch (err) {
+      // Stale tokens (registration-token-not-registered) are common when
+      // a customer reinstalls the app. Don't escalate; just count and
+      // continue.
+      logger.warn('Deactivation FCM send failed', {
+        shopId: context.shopId,
+        transition: context.transition,
+        error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
+      });
+    }
+  }
+  return sent;
+}
+

codex
The new token-based Decision Circle flow transfers project ownership away from the original customer, and the occasion rename silently degrades existing persisted customer-memory data. There is also a user-facing mismatch between the new 30-day deactivation grace period and the still-24-hour UI copy.

Full review comments:

- [P1] Keep token-based joins from transferring project ownership — C:\Alok\Business Projects\Almira-Project\functions\src\join_decision_circle.ts:262-267
  When `joinToken` is present this code path is now documented as a participant add, but it still rewrites `projects/{projectId}.customerUid` from `sourceUid` to `destUid`. That breaks the existing access model in `firestore.rules`, where the original customer can only read their own projects, so a customer who shares a Decision Circle link will lose access to their own order as soon as the join completes. This only affects the new token-backed join flow; legacy full-account merges are fine.

- [P1] Preserve legacy `dahej` values when renaming occasions — C:\Alok\Business Projects\Almira-Project\packages\lib_core\lib\src\models\customer_memory.dart:24-28
  Older customer-memory documents were written with the wire value `dahej`. After this enum rename, those stored values no longer map to a real `PreferredOccasion`, and `CustomerMemory.fromJson` will fall back to `PreferredOccasion.other`, silently dropping the saved occasion whenever an existing record is read and then re-saved. This affects any shop that already has customer-memory data, so the rename needs a compatibility alias or a data migration.

- [P2] Update operator-facing deactivation copy with the new 30-day grace — C:\Alok\Business Projects\Almira-Project\functions\src\shop_deactivation_sweep.ts:48-48
  This changes the backend grace period from 24 hours to 30 days, but the app strings still tell operators they can reverse shop closure only “in the next 24 hours” (`shopClosureReversibilityFooter` in both locale files). After this lands, the deactivation flow will present the wrong deadline in every environment, which is especially risky for an irreversible lifecycle action.
The new token-based Decision Circle flow transfers project ownership away from the original customer, and the occasion rename silently degrades existing persisted customer-memory data. There is also a user-facing mismatch between the new 30-day deactivation grace period and the still-24-hour UI copy.

Full review comments:

- [P1] Keep token-based joins from transferring project ownership — C:\Alok\Business Projects\Almira-Project\functions\src\join_decision_circle.ts:262-267
  When `joinToken` is present this code path is now documented as a participant add, but it still rewrites `projects/{projectId}.customerUid` from `sourceUid` to `destUid`. That breaks the existing access model in `firestore.rules`, where the original customer can only read their own projects, so a customer who shares a Decision Circle link will lose access to their own order as soon as the join completes. This only affects the new token-backed join flow; legacy full-account merges are fine.

- [P1] Preserve legacy `dahej` values when renaming occasions — C:\Alok\Business Projects\Almira-Project\packages\lib_core\lib\src\models\customer_memory.dart:24-28
  Older customer-memory documents were written with the wire value `dahej`. After this enum rename, those stored values no longer map to a real `PreferredOccasion`, and `CustomerMemory.fromJson` will fall back to `PreferredOccasion.other`, silently dropping the saved occasion whenever an existing record is read and then re-saved. This affects any shop that already has customer-memory data, so the rename needs a compatibility alias or a data migration.

- [P2] Update operator-facing deactivation copy with the new 30-day grace — C:\Alok\Business Projects\Almira-Project\functions\src\shop_deactivation_sweep.ts:48-48
  This changes the backend grace period from 24 hours to 30 days, but the app strings still tell operators they can reverse shop closure only “in the next 24 hours” (`shopClosureReversibilityFooter` in both locale files). After this lands, the deactivation flow will present the wrong deadline in every environment, which is especially risky for an irreversible lifecycle action.
